## ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços

```markdown
# ADR-001: Arquitetura Baseada em Microsserviços

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Arquitetura Squad

## CONTEXTO:
DIYAPP V10 precisa escalar para 100k usuários ativos com 99.9% de disponibilidade.
O sistema monolítico atual tem:
- Acoplamento alto entre funcionalidades
- Tempos de deploy longos (> 30min)
- Dificuldade de escalar componentes específicos
- Single point of failure

## DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
1. Cada serviço é responsável por um domínio de negócio específico
2. Comunicação via API REST com fallback para mensageria
3. Banco de dados por serviço (Database per Service)
4. API Gateway como ponto único de entrada
5. Observabilidade centralizada

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A:** Monolito modularizado - Prós: Simples, consistência transacional. Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, deploy único.
- **Opção B:** Microsserviços completos - Prós: Escalabilidade independente, resiliência. Contras: Complexidade operacional, consistência eventual.
- **Opção C:** Arquitetura híbrida - Prós: Balanceamento. Contras: Gerenciamento complexo.

**Opção escolhida:** B - Justificativa: Alinhamento com metas de escala e disponibilidade.

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Escalabilidade granular por serviço
- Deploys independentes e rápidos
- Resiliência melhorada (fallback por serviço)
- Equipes autônomas por serviço

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade de operações distribuídas
- Consistência eventual em alguns casos
- Overhead de comunicação entre serviços
- Monitoramento distribuído necessário

**Riscos:**
- Latência em chamadas entre serviços
- Mitigação: Cache estratégico, timeouts configuráveis
- Debug distribuído complexo
- Mitigação: Correlation IDs, logging centralizado

## REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15
```

## Engineering Standards

```markdown
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V10

## 1. Padrões de Código

### 1.1 JavaScript/TypeScript
- TypeScript estrito (strict: true)
- ESLint com Airbnb Base
- Prettier para formatação
- Testes: Jest + Supertest
- Cobertura mínima: 80%

### 1.2 Estrutura de Serviço
```
service-name/
├── src/
│   ├── controllers/
│   ├── services/
│   ├── models/
│   ├── repositories/
│   ├── middleware/
│   ├── utils/
│   ├── config/
│   ├── routes.ts
│   └── app.ts
├── tests/
│   ├── unit/
│   ├── integration/
│   └── fixtures/
└── package.json
```

### 1.3 API Design
- RESTful com versionamento (v1/, v2/)
- JSON como formato padrão
- Error response padrão:
```json
{
  "error": {
    "code": "VALIDATION_ERROR",
    "message": "Invalid input",
    "details": [...]
  }
}
```

### 1.4 Banco de Dados
- PostgreSQL para dados transacionais
- Redis para cache e sessões
- Migrations versionadas
- Índices para queries frequentes

## 2. Convenções de Git

### 2.1 Branching Strategy
- `main`: produção
- `develop`: integração
- `feature/*`: novas funcionalidades
- `hotfix/*`: correções urgentes
- `release/*`: preparação de release

### 2.2 Conventional Commits
```
feat: add user authentication
fix: resolve memory leak in image processing
docs: update API documentation
style: format code with prettier
refactor: simplify payment service
test: add unit tests for validation
chore: update dependencies
```

### 2.3 Pull Requests
- Título descritivo
- Descrição com contexto
- Link para issue/ticket
- Review obrigatório do Tech Lead
- Todos os testes passando
- Cobertura mantida ou melhorada

## 3. Segurança

### 3.1 Autenticação/Autorização
- JWT com expiração curta (15min)
- Refresh tokens com revogação
- Rate limiting por IP/serviço
- Input validation em todas as APIs

### 3.2 Dados Sensíveis
- Nunca logar dados sensíveis
- Hash com bcrypt para senhas
- Secrets em variáveis de ambiente
- Criptografia em trânsito (TLS 1.3)

## 4. Performance

### 4.1 Otimizações
- Cache estratégico (Redis)
- Paginação em listagens grandes
- Connection pooling para DB
- Compressão Gzip/Brotli

### 4.2 Monitoring
- Health checks em /health
- Métricas Prometheus
- Logs estruturados (JSON)
- Tracing distribuído (Jaeger)

## 5. Containerização

### 5.1 Docker
- Imagens Alpine-based
- Multi-stage builds
- Non-root users
- Health checks configurados

### 5.2 Kubernetes
- Resource limits definidos
- Liveness/readiness probes
- Horizontal Pod Autoscaling
- ConfigMaps para configuração
```

## Docker Compose para Desenvolvimento

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # API Gateway
  api-gateway:
    build: ./src/api-gateway
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - AUTH_SERVICE_URL=http://auth-service:3001
      - PROJECT_SERVICE_URL=http://project-service:3002
    depends_on:
      - auth-service
      - project-service
    volumes:
      - ./src/api-gateway:/app
      - /app/node_modules

  # Auth Service
  auth-service:
    build: ./src/auth-service
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - DB_HOST=auth-db
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
    depends_on:
      - auth-db
      - redis
    volumes:
      - ./src/auth-service:/app
      - /app/node_modules

  # Project Service
  project-service:
    build: ./src/project-service
    ports:
      - "3002:3002"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - DB_HOST=project-db
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
    depends_on:
      - project-db
      - redis
    volumes:
      - ./src/project-service:/app
      - /app/node_modules

  # Databases
  auth-db:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=auth_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=admin
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=secret
    volumes:
      - auth-db-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"

  project-db:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=project_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=admin
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=secret
    volumes:
      - project-db-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    ports:
      - "5433:5432"

  # Redis
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"

  # Monitoring
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=admin
    ports:
      - "3003:3000"
    volumes:
      - ./infrastructure/monitoring/grafana-dashboards:/var/lib/grafana/dashboards

volumes:
  auth-db-data:
  project-db-data:
```

## Pipeline CI/CD (.github/workflows/ci-pipeline.yml)

```yaml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main, develop ]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, auth-service, project-service, notification-service]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        cache: 'npm'
        cache-dependency-path: src/${{ matrix.service }}/package-lock.json
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      working-directory: src/${{ matrix.service }}
      run: npm ci
    
    - name: Lint
      working-directory: src/${{ matrix.service }}
      run: npm run lint
    
    - name: Run tests
      working-directory: src/${{ matrix.service }}
      run: npm test -- --coverage
    
    - name: Upload coverage
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: src/${{ matrix.service }}/coverage/coverage-final.json
        flags: ${{ matrix.service }}
        name: codecov-umbrella

  security-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Run Snyk to check for vulnerabilities
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --severity-threshold=high
    
    - name: Run Trivy vulnerability scanner
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        scan-type: 'fs'
        scan-ref: '.'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
    
    - name: Upload Trivy scan results to GitHub Security tab
      uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
      with:
        sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'

  build-containers:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [test, security-scan]
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, auth-service, project-service, notification-service]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Set up Docker Buildx
      uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
    
    - name: Login to DockerHub
      uses: docker/login-action@v2
      with:
        username: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}
        password: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_PASSWORD }}
    
    - name: Build and push
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
      with:
        context: ./src/${{ matrix.service }}
        push: true
        tags: |
          ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/${{ matrix.service }}:latest
          ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/${{ matrix.service }}:${{ github.sha }}
        cache-from: type=gha
        cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
```

## Dockerfile Template para Serviços

```dockerfile
# Build stage
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Copy package files
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source
COPY . .

# Build TypeScript
RUN npm run build

# Production stage
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Create non-root user
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001

# Copy built application
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --chown=nodejs:nodejs package*.json ./

# Switch to non-root user
USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node -e "require('http').get('http://localhost:${PORT}/health', (r) => {if(r.statusCode !== 200) throw new Error()})"

# Expose port
EXPOSE ${PORT:-3000}

# Start application
CMD ["node", "dist/app.js"]
```

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Design e UI

## Estrutura do Projeto

## 1. Design Tokens (design-tokens.js)

```javascript
// design-tokens.js
class DesignTokens {
  constructor() {
    this.mode = this.getPreferredColorScheme();
    this.init();
  }

  getPreferredColorScheme() {
    if (window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches) {
      return 'dark';
    }
    return 'light';
  }

  init() {
    this.tokens = {
      colors: {
        light: {
          primary: {
            50: '#f0f9ff',
            100: '#e0f2fe',
            200: '#bae6fd',
            300: '#7dd3fc',
            400: '#38bdf8',
            500: '#0ea5e9',
            600: '#0284c7',
            700: '#0369a1',
            800: '#075985',
            900: '#0c4a6e'
          },
          neutral: {
            50: '#fafafa',
            100: '#f5f5f5',
            200: '#e5e5e5',
            300: '#d4d4d4',
            400: '#a3a3a3',
            500: '#737373',
            600: '#525252',
            700: '#404040',
            800: '#262626',
            900: '#171717'
          },
          semantic: {
            success: '#10b981',
            warning: '#f59e0b',
            error: '#ef4444',
            info: '#3b82f6'
          },
          background: {
            primary: '#ffffff',
            secondary: '#f8fafc',
            tertiary: '#f1f5f9'
          },
          surface: {
            default: '#ffffff',
            elevated: '#ffffff',
            overlay: '#ffffff'
          }
        },
        dark: {
          primary: {
            50: '#0c4a6e',
            100: '#075985',
            200: '#0369a1',
            300: '#0284c7',
            400: '#0ea5e9',
            500: '#38bdf8',
            600: '#7dd3fc',
            700: '#bae6fd',
            800: '#e0f2fe',
            900: '#f0f9ff'
          },
          neutral: {
            50: '#171717',
            100: '#262626',
            200: '#404040',
            300: '#525252',
            400: '#737373',
            500: '#a3a3a3',
            600: '#d4d4d4',
            700: '#e5e5e5',
            800: '#f5f5f5',
            900: '#fafafa'
          },
          semantic: {
            success: '#34d399',
            warning: '#fbbf24',
            error: '#f87171',
            info: '#60a5fa'
          },
          background: {
            primary: '#0f172a',
            secondary: '#1e293b',
            tertiary: '#334155'
          },
          surface: {
            default: '#1e293b',
            elevated: '#334155',
            overlay: '#475569'
          }
        }
      },
      typography: {
        fontFamily: {
          sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
          mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'Courier New', monospace"
        },
        fontSize: {
          xs: '0.75rem',
          sm: '0.875rem',
          base: '1rem',
          lg: '1.125rem',
          xl: '1.25rem',
          '2xl': '1.5rem',
          '3xl': '1.875rem',
          '4xl': '2.25rem',
          '5xl': '3rem'
        },
        fontWeight: {
          normal: '400',
          medium: '500',
          semibold: '600',
          bold: '700'
        },
        lineHeight: {
          tight: '1.25',
          normal: '1.5',
          relaxed: '1.75'
        }
      },
      spacing: {
        px: '1px',
        0: '0',
        0.5: '0.125rem',
        1: '0.25rem',
        1.5: '0.375rem',
        2: '0.5rem',
        2.5: '0.625rem',
        3: '0.75rem',
        3.5: '0.875rem',
        4: '1rem',
        5: '1.25rem',
        6: '1.5rem',
        7: '1.75rem',
        8: '2rem',
        9: '2.25rem',
        10: '2.5rem',
        12: '3rem',
        14: '3.5rem',
        16: '4rem',
        20: '5rem',
        24: '6rem',
        28: '7rem',
        32: '8rem'
      },
      borderRadius: {
        none: '0',
        sm: '0.125rem',
        base: '0.25rem',
        md: '0.375rem',
        lg: '0.5rem',
        xl: '0.75rem',
        '2xl': '1rem',
        '3xl': '1.5rem',
        full: '9999px'
      },
      shadows: {
        sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
        base: '0 1px 3px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
        md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
        lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
        xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04)',
        '2xl': '0 25px 50px -12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.25)',
        inner: 'inset 0 2px 4px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)'
      },
      transitions: {
        duration: {
          fast: '150ms',
          normal: '300ms',
          slow: '500ms'
        },
        easing: {
          linear: 'linear',
          in: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)',
          out: 'cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)',
          inOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)'
        }
      },
      zIndex: {
        hide: -1,
        base: 0,
        docked: 10,
        dropdown: 1000,
        sticky: 1100,
        banner: 1200,
        overlay: 1300,
        modal: 1400,
        popover: 1500,
        skipLink: 1600,
        toast: 1700,
        tooltip: 1800
      }
    };

    this.applyTokens();
    this.setupThemeToggle();
  }

  applyTokens() {
    const root = document.documentElement;
    const colors = this.tokens.colors[this.mode];
    
    // Apply color tokens
    Object.entries(colors).forEach(([category, values]) => {
      Object.entries(values).forEach(([key, value]) => {
        if (typeof value === 'object') {
          Object.entries(value).forEach(([shade, color]) => {
            root.style.setProperty(`--color-${category}-${key}-${shade}`, color);
          });
        } else {
          root.style.setProperty(`--color-${category}-${key}`, value);
        }
      });
    });

    // Apply typography
    Object.entries(this.tokens.typography).forEach(([category, values]) => {
      if (typeof values === 'object') {
        Object.entries(values).forEach(([key, value]) => {
          root.style.setProperty(`--font-${category}-${key}`, value);
        });
      } else {
        root.style.setProperty(`--font-${category}`, values);
      }
    });

    // Apply spacing
    Object.entries(this.tokens.spacing).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--spacing-${key}`, value);
    });

    // Apply other tokens
    Object.entries(this.tokens.borderRadius).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--radius-${key}`, value);
    });

    Object.entries(this.tokens.shadows).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--shadow-${key}`, value);
    });

    // Set mode attribute for CSS targeting
    root.setAttribute('data-theme', this.mode);
  }

  setupThemeToggle() {
    const toggle = document.createElement('button');
    toggle.id = 'theme-toggle';
    toggle.className = 'theme-toggle';
    toggle.innerHTML = this.mode === 'dark' ? '☀️' : '🌙';
    toggle.setAttribute('aria-label', `Switch to ${this.mode === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark'} mode`);
    
    toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
      this.mode = this.mode === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark';
      this.applyTokens();
      toggle.innerHTML = this.mode === 'dark' ? '☀️' : '🌙';
      toggle.setAttribute('aria-label', `Switch to ${this.mode === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark'} mode`);
      
      // Save preference
      localStorage.setItem('diyapp-theme', this.mode);
    });

    // Load saved preference
    const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('diyapp-theme');
    if (savedTheme) {
      this.mode = savedTheme;
      this.applyTokens();
      toggle.innerHTML = this.mode === 'dark' ? '☀️' : '🌙';
    }

    document.body.appendChild(toggle);
  }

  getToken(category, ...path) {
    let value = this.tokens[category];
    for (const key of path) {
      if (value && typeof value === 'object' && key in value) {
        value = value[key];
      } else {
        console.warn(`Token not found: ${category}.${path.join('.')}`);
        return null;
      }
    }
    return value;
  }
}

// Initialize design tokens
window.designTokens = new DesignTokens();
```

## 1. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Redis para cache, sessões e filas
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-StrongPassword123!}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "--raw", "incr", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Core Service (API Gateway + Auth)
  core-service:
    build: ./core-service
    container_name: diyapp-core
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - PORT=3000
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET:-your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production}
      - JWT_EXPIRES_IN=24h
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - REDIS_PORT=6379
      - REDIS_PASSWORD=${REDIS_PASSWORD:-StrongPassword123!}
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS=900000
      - RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS=100
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./core-service/logs:/app/logs
      - ./shared:/app/shared
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # Automation Service
  automation-service:
    build: ./automation-service
    container_name: diyapp-automation
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - PORT=3001
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - REDIS_PORT=6379
      - REDIS_PASSWORD=${REDIS_PASSWORD:-StrongPassword123!}
      - WORKER_CONCURRENCY=5
      - TASK_TIMEOUT_MS=300000
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./automation-service/logs:/app/logs
      - ./shared:/app/shared
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3001/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # Nginx como load balancer (opcional)
  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    container_name: diyapp-nginx
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
    depends_on:
      - core-service
      - automation-service
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

volumes:
  redis_data:

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
```

### 2.2 core-service/src/index.js

```javascript
require('express-async-errors');
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const compression = require('compression');
const config = require('./config');
const logger = require('./utils/logger');
const authRoutes = require('./routes/auth');
const apiRoutes = require('./routes/api');
const { errorHandler, notFoundHandler } = require('./middleware/errorHandler');

const app = express();

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
    },
  },
}));

app.use(cors({
  origin: config.cors.origin,
  credentials: true,
}));

app.use(compression());
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Request logging middleware
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || require('uuid').v4();
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  res.setHeader('X-Correlation-ID', correlationId);
  
  const start = Date.now();
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    logger.info({
      correlationId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      status: res.statusCode,
      duration,
      userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip,
    }, 'HTTP Request');
  });
  
  next();
});

// Routes
app.use('/auth', authRoutes);
app.use('/api', apiRoutes);

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    service: 'core-service',
    uptime: process.uptime(),
  });
});

// Dashboard
app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(__dirname + '/public/index.html');
});

// Error handling
app.use(notFoundHandler);
app.use(errorHandler);

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  logger.info('SIGTERM received, starting graceful shutdown');
  server.close(() => {
    logger.info('HTTP server closed');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

const server = app.listen(config.port, () => {
  logger.info(`Core Service running on port ${config.port}`);
});

module.exports = app;
```

  port: process.env.PORT || 3000,
  nodeEnv: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',

    expiresIn: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h',
    algorithm: 'HS256',
  },
  
  redis: {
    host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT || '6379'),
    password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
    tls: process.env.REDIS_TLS === 'true',
    keyPrefix: 'core:',
  },
  
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS || '900000'), // 15 minutes
    maxRequests: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS || '100'),
  },

    origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || '*',
  },
  
  services: {
    automation: {
      url: process.env.AUTOMATION_SERVICE_URL || 'http://automation-service:3001',
      timeout: parseInt(process.env.SERVICE_TIMEOUT || '5000'),
    },

    resetTimeout: 30000,
    timeout: 5000,
  },
};

### 2.4 core-service/src/middleware/auth.js

```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const config = require('../config');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const redisService = require('../services/redisService');

class AuthenticationError extends Error {
  constructor(message, code = 'AUTH_ERROR') {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'AuthenticationError';
    this.code = code;
    this.statusCode = 401;
  }
}

class AuthorizationError extends Error {
  constructor(message, code = 'FORBIDDEN') {
    super(message);
    this.name = 'AuthorizationError';
    this.code = code;
    this.statusCode = 403;
  }
}

const authenticate = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
    
    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      throw new AuthenticationError('No token provided', 'NO_TOKEN');
    }
    
    const token = authHeader.substring(7);
    
    // Check token blacklist
    const isBlacklisted = await redisService.isTokenBlacklisted(token);
    if (isBlacklisted) {
      throw new AuthenticationError('Token has been revoked', 'TOKEN_REVOKED');
    }
    
    // Verify JWT
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, config.jwt.secret, {
      algorithms: [config.jwt.algorithm],
    });
    
    // Attach user to request
    req.user = {
      id: decoded.sub,
      email: decoded.email,
      roles: decoded.roles || ['user'],
      permissions: decoded.permissions || [],
    };
    
    // Add to request context for logging
    req.userId = decoded.sub;
    
    logger.debug({
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
      userId: decoded.sub,
      action: 'authenticate',
    }, 'User authenticated');
    
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    if (error.name === 'JsonWebTokenError') {
      next(new AuthenticationError('Invalid token', 'INVALID_TOKEN'));
    } else if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
      next(new AuthenticationError('Token expired', 'TOKEN_EXPIRED'));
    } else {
      next(error);
    }
  }
};

const authorize = (requiredPermissions = []) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    try {
      if (!req.user) {
        throw new AuthenticationError('Authentication required');
      }
      
      if (requiredPermissions.length === 0) {
        return next();
      }
      
      const userPermissions = req.user.permissions || [];
      const hasPermission = requiredPermissions.some(permission => 
        userPermissions.includes(permission)
      );
      
      if (!hasPermission) {
        logger.warn({
          correlationId: req.correlationId,
          userId: req.user.id,
          requiredPermissions,
          userPermissions,
          path: req.path,
        }, 'Authorization failed');
        
        throw new AuthorizationError('Insufficient permissions');
      }
      
      next();
    } catch (error) {
      next(error);
    }
  };
};

const requireRole = (requiredRoles = []) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    try {
      if (!req.user) {
        throw new AuthenticationError('Authentication required');
      }
      
      if (requiredRoles.length === 0) {
        return next();
      }
      
      const userRoles = req.user.roles || [];
      const hasRole = requiredRoles.some(role => 
        userRoles.includes(role)
      );
      
      if (!hasRole) {
        logger.warn({
          correlationId: req.correlationId,
          userId: req.user.id,
          requiredRoles,
          userRoles,
          path: req.path,
        }, 'Role check failed');
        
        throw new AuthorizationError('Insufficient role');
      }
      
      next();
    } catch (error) {
      next(error);
    }
  };
};

module.exports = {
  authenticate,
  authorize,
  requireRole,
  AuthenticationError,
  AuthorizationError,
};
```

### 2.5 core-service/src/middleware/rateLimiter.js

```javascript
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const RedisStore = require('rate-limit-redis');
const config = require('../config');
const redisService = require('../services/redisService');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

// Global rate limiter
const globalLimiter = rateLimit({
  store: new RedisStore({
    sendCommand: (...args) => redisService.client.sendCommand(args),
    prefix: 'rate-limit:global:',
  }),
  windowMs: config.rateLimit.windowMs,
  max: config.rateLimit.maxRequests,
  message: {
    error: 'Too many requests',
    code: 'RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED',
    retryAfter: config.rateLimit.windowMs / 1000,
  },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  skip: (req) => {
    // Skip rate limiting for health checks
    return req.path === '/health';
  },
  handler: (req, res, next, options) => {
    logger.warn({
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
      ip: req.ip,
      path: req.path,
      limit: options.max,
      windowMs: options.windowMs,
    }, 'Rate limit exceeded');
    
    res.status(429).json(options.message);
  },
});

// Stricter rate limiter for auth endpoints
const authLimiter = rateLimit({
  store: new RedisStore({
    sendCommand: (...args) => redisService.client.sendCommand(args),
    prefix: 'rate-limit:auth:',
  }),
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 5, // 5 attempts per window
  message: {
    error: 'Too many authentication attempts',
    code: 'AUTH_RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED',
    retryAfter: 15 * 60,
  },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  skipSuccessfulRequests: true, // Don't count successful auth
});

// Dynamic rate limiter based on user tier
const tieredLimiter = (tierConfig) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    const userTier = req.user?.tier || 'free';
    const config = tierConfig[userTier] || tierConfig.free;
    


### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Dashboard SPA

## 1. Configuração Inicial

**package.json**
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v10-dashboard",
  "version": "1.0.0",

```typescript
import React from 'react';
import { designTokens } from '@/styles/design-tokens';
import clsx from 'clsx';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

const Button = React.forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      isLoading = false,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      fullWidth = false,
      className,
      disabled,
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const baseStyles = {
      display: 'inline-flex',
      alignItems: 'center',
      justifyContent: 'center',
      fontWeight: designTokens.typography.fontWeight.medium,
      fontFamily: designTokens.typography.fontFamily.primary,
      border: 'none',
      borderRadius: designTokens.borders.radius.base,
      cursor: 'pointer',
      transition: `all ${designTokens.transitions.duration.fast} ${designTokens.transitions.timing.ease}`,
      outline: 'none',
      width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
      position: 'relative',
      '&:disabled': {
        cursor: 'not-allowed',
        opacity: 0.6,
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${designTokens.colors.primary[200]}`,
      },
    };

    const variantStyles = {
      primary: {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[600],
        color: 'white',
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[700],
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.primary[800],
        },
      },
      secondary: {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[200],
        color: designTokens.colors.neutral[800],
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[300],
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[400],
        },
      },
      outline: {
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        color: designTokens.colors.neutral[700],
        border: `${designTokens.borders.width.thin} solid ${designTokens.colors.neutral[300]}`,
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[50],
          borderColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[400],
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[100],
        },
      },
      ghost: {
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',

        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {

        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.neutral[200],
        },
      },
      danger: {
        backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.error[600],
        color: 'white',
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.error[700],
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: designTokens.colors.error[800],
        },
      },
    };

    const sizeStyles = {
      sm: {
        fontSize: designTokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
        padding: `${designTokens.spacing[1]} ${designTokens.spacing[3]}`,
        gap: designTokens.spacing[1],
        minHeight: '2rem',

      md: {
        fontSize: designTokens.typ

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Data Engineering Implementation

## 1. Database Schema Design (PostgreSQL + TimescaleDB)

```sql
-- File: database/schema.sql
-- PostgreSQL 14+ with TimescaleDB extension

-- Enable TimescaleDB extension
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS timescaledb;

-- ======================
-- CORE TABLES (Raw/Bronze Layer)
-- ======================

-- Raw event data from all sources
CREATE TABLE raw_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    source_system VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_data JSONB NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'
);

-- Raw LLM API calls from gateway
CREATE TABLE raw_llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    endpoint VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    request_body JSONB NOT NULL,
    response_body JSONB,
    status_code INTEGER,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER,
    completion_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    called_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Raw infrastructure metrics
CREATE TABLE raw_infra_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_value DECIMAL(15,4) NOT NULL,
    metric_unit VARCHAR(20),
    resource_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    resource_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    tags JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    collected_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ======================
-- HYPER TABLES (TimescaleDB optimized)
-- ======================

-- User events hyper table (time-series optimized)
CREATE TABLE user_events (
    event_time TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    user_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_properties JSONB,
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    platform VARCHAR(20),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    session_id VARCHAR(100)
);

SELECT create_hypertable('user_events', 'event_time',
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '1 day',
    create_default_indexes => FALSE
);

-- Create optimized indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_user_events_user_time ON user_events(user_id, event_time DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_events_name_time ON user_events(event_name, event_time DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_events_properties ON user_events USING GIN(event_properties);

-- LLM performance metrics hyper table
CREATE TABLE llm_performance (
    timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    avg_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p95_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p99_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    total_calls INTEGER,
    success_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(12,6),
    error_count INTEGER
);

SELECT create_hypertable('llm_performance', 'timestamp',
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '1 hour',
    create_default_indexes => FALSE
);

CREATE INDEX idx_llm_perf_provider_model ON llm_performance(provider, model, timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_llm_perf_feature ON llm_performance(feature_name, timestamp DESC);

-- Infrastructure monitoring hyper table
CREATE TABLE infra_monitoring (
    timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    resource_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    avg_value DECIMAL(15,4),
    max_value DECIMAL(15,4),
    min_value DECIMAL(15,4),
    sample_count INTEGER
);

SELECT create_hypertable('infra_monitoring', 'timestamp',
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '5 minutes',
    create_default_indexes => FALSE
);

CREATE INDEX idx_infra_monitoring_metric ON infra_monitoring(metric_name, timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_infra_monitoring_resource ON infra_monitoring(resource_id, timestamp DESC);

-- ======================
-- DIMENSION TABLES (Silver Layer)
-- ======================

-- Users dimension
CREATE TABLE dim_users (
    user_id VARCHAR(100) PRIMARY KEY,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    last_seen_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    total_sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    first_app_version VARCHAR(20),
    last_app_version VARCHAR(20),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    user_segment VARCHAR(50),
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Features dimension
CREATE TABLE dim_features (
    feature_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    feature_category VARCHAR(50),
    description TEXT,
    launched_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    owner_team VARCHAR(50)
);

-- LLM models dimension
CREATE TABLE dim_llm_models (
    model_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    context_window INTEGER,
    max_tokens INTEGER,
    input_cost_per_1k DECIMAL(10,6),
    output_cost_per_1k DECIMAL(10,6),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    supported_features JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
    UNIQUE(provider, model_name)
);

-- ======================
-- FACT TABLES (Gold/Marts Layer)
-- ======================

-- Product metrics fact table
CREATE TABLE fact_product_metrics (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    hour INTEGER,
    feature_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_features(feature_id),
    metric_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    metric_value DECIMAL(15,4) NOT NULL,
    breakdown JSONB,
    computed_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    PRIMARY KEY (date, hour, feature_id, metric_name)
);

-- LLM cost fact table
CREATE TABLE fact_llm_costs (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_llm_models(model_id),
    feature_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_features(feature_id),
    total_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    prompt_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    completion_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(12,6) NOT NULL,
    avg_cost_per_call_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    call_count INTEGER NOT NULL,
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    computed_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    PRIMARY KEY (date, provider, model_id, feature_id)
);

-- User engagement fact table
CREATE TABLE fact_user_engagement (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    user_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    feature_id INTEGER REFERENCES dim_features(feature_id),
    session_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    event_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_duration_seconds INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    last_event_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    computed_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    PRIMARY KEY (date, user_id, feature_id)
);

-- ======================
-- RETENTION POLICIES
-- ======================

-- Raw data retention: 90 days
SELECT add_retention_policy('raw_events', INTERVAL '90 days');
SELECT add_retention_policy('raw_llm_calls', INTERVAL '90 days');
SELECT add_retention_policy('raw_infra_metrics', INTERVAL '90 days');

-- Hyper tables retention
SELECT add_retention_policy('user_events', INTERVAL '30 days');
SELECT add_retention_policy('llm_performance', INTERVAL '60 days');
SELECT add_retention_policy('infra_monitoring', INTERVAL '7 days');

-- ======================
-- VIEWS FOR COMMON QUERIES
-- ======================

CREATE VIEW vw_daily_active_users AS
SELECT 
    date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as dau,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN session_count > 0 THEN user_id END) as engaged_users
FROM fact_user_engagement
GROUP BY date
ORDER BY date DESC;

CREATE VIEW vw_feature_adoption AS
SELECT 
    f.feature_name,
    f.feature_category,
    COUNT(DISTINCT ue.user_id) as total_users,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN ue.date = CURRENT_DATE THEN ue.user_id END) as daily_users,
    AVG(ue.event_count) as avg_events_per_user,
    SUM(ue.event_count) as total_events
FROM fact_user_engagement ue
JOIN dim_features f ON ue.feature_id = f.feature_id
WHERE f.is_active = TRUE
GROUP BY f.feature_id, f.feature_name, f.feature_category;

CREATE VIEW vw_llm_cost_by_feature AS
SELECT 
    fc.date,
    f.feature_name,
    m.provider,
    m.model_name,
    fc.total_cost_usd,
    fc.total_tokens,
    fc.call_count,
    fc.avg_cost_per_call_usd,
    ROUND(fc.total_cost_usd / SUM(fc.total_cost_usd) OVER (PARTITION BY fc.date) * 100, 2) as cost_percentage
FROM fact_llm_costs fc
JOIN dim_features f ON fc.feature_id = f.feature_id
JOIN dim_llm_models m ON fc.model_id = m.model_id
ORDER BY fc.date DESC, fc.total_cost_usd DESC;

-- File: database/init_performance.sql
-- Performance optimizations

-- Enable query parallelism
SET max_parallel_workers_per_gather = 4;
SET parallel_setup_cost = 100;
SET parallel_tuple_cost = 0.1;

-- Create materialized views for frequent queries
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW mv_daily_metrics_summary AS
SELECT 
    date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as active_users,
    SUM(session_count) as total_sessions,
    SUM(event_count) as total_events,
    COUNT(DISTINCT feature_id) as active_features
FROM fact_user_engagement
GROUP BY date
WITH DATA;

-- Refresh schedule for materialized view
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION refresh_daily_metrics()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    REFRESH MATERIALIZED VIEW CONCURRENTLY mv_daily_metrics_summary;
    RETURN NULL;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Create indexes for performance
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_events_timestamp ON raw_events(event_timestamp DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_calls_called_at ON raw_llm_calls(called_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_calls_feature ON raw_llm_calls(feature_name, called_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_product_metrics_date ON fact_product_metrics(date DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_fact_llm_costs_date ON fact_llm_costs(date DESC);

-- Create partial indexes for active data
CREATE INDEX idx_active_features ON dim_features(feature_id) WHERE is_active = TRUE;
CREATE INDEX idx_active_llm_models ON dim_llm_models(model_id) WHERE is_active = TRUE;
```

## 2. ETL Pipeline Implementation (dbt + Python)

```yaml
# File: dbt_project.yml
name: 'diyapp_v10'
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'diyapp_v10'

model-paths: ["models"]
analysis-paths: ["analyses"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
seed-paths: ["seeds"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_v10:
    materialized: table
    staging:
      materialized: view
      +schema: staging
    marts:
      materialized: table
      +schema: marts
      product:
        +schema: marts_product
      ai:
        +schema: marts_ai
      ops:
        +schema: marts_ops

seeds:
  diyapp_v10:
    +schema: seeds
    +enabled: true
```

```sql
-- File: models/staging/stg_events.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='view',
    schema='staging'
) }}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT 
        event_id,
        source_system,
        event_type,
        event_data,
        event_timestamp,
        ingested_at,
        metadata
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'raw_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '90 days'
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    source_system,
    LOWER(event_type) as event_type,
    event_data->>'user_id' as user_id,
    event_data->>'session_id' as session_id,
    event_data->>'feature' as feature_name,
    event_data->>'app_version' as app_version,
    event_data->>'platform' as platform,
    event_data->>'country' as country_code,
    event_data->>'duration'::DECIMAL as duration_seconds,
    event_timestamp,
    ingested_at,
    event_data as event_properties,
    metadata
FROM raw_events
WHERE event_data->>'user_id' IS NOT NULL
  AND event_timestamp IS NOT NULL

-- File: models/staging/stg_llm_calls.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='view',
    schema='staging'
) }}

SELECT
    call_id,
    LOWER(provider) as provider,
    LOWER(model) as model,
    endpoint,
    request_body,
    response_body,
    status_code,
    COALESCE(prompt_tokens, 0) as prompt_tokens,
    COALESCE(completion_tokens, 0) as completion_tokens,
    COALESCE(total_tokens, 0) as total_tokens,
    COALESCE(latency_ms, 0) as latency_ms,
    COALESCE(cost_usd, 0) as cost_usd,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    LOWER(feature_name) as feature_name,
    called_at,
    ingested_at,
    CASE 
        WHEN status_code BETWEEN 200 AND 299 THEN 'success'
        WHEN status_code BETWEEN 400 AND 499 THEN 'client_error'
        WHEN status_code BETWEEN 500 AND 599 THEN 'server_error'
        ELSE 'unknown'
    END as call_status
FROM {{ source('raw', 'raw_llm_calls') }}
WHERE called_at >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '90 days'
  AND feature_name IS NOT NULL

-- File: models/marts/product/daily_active_users.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    schema='marts_product',
    tags=['product', 'metrics']
) }}

WITH daily_events AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) as event_date,
        user_id,
        COUNT(*) as event_count,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as session_count,
        MAX(event_timestamp) as last_event_time
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

feature_usage AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(e.event_timestamp) as event_date,
        e.user_id,
        COALESCE(f.feature_id, 0) as feature_id,
        COUNT(*) as feature_event_count
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }} e
    LEFT JOIN {{ ref('dim_features') }} f 
        ON LOWER(e.feature_name) = LOWER(f.feature_name)
    WHERE e.feature_name IS NOT NULL
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
)

SELECT
    de.event_date as date,
    de.user_id,
    de.event_count,
    de.session_count,
    de.last_event_time,
    fu.feature_id,
    COALESCE(fu.feature_event_count, 0) as feature_event_count,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP as computed_at
FROM daily_events de
LEFT JOIN feature_usage fu 
    ON de.event_date = fu.event_date 
    AND de.user_id = fu.user_id
WHERE de.event_count > 0

-- File: models/marts/ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    schema='marts_ai',
    tags=['ai', 'cost', 'llm']
) }}

WITH daily_llm_calls AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(called_at) as call_date,
        provider,
        model,
        feature_name,
        COUNT(*) as call_count,
        SUM(prompt_tokens) as total_prompt_tokens,
        SUM(completion_tokens) as total_completion_tokens,
        SUM(total_tokens) as total_tokens,
        SUM(cost_usd) as total_cost_usd,
        AVG(cost_usd) as avg_cost_per_call,
        SUM(CASE WHEN call_status != 'success' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as error_count
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_calls') }}
    WHERE called_at >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '60 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

model_mapping AS (
    SELECT
        dlc.*,
        COALESCE(dm.model_id, 0) as model_id,
        COALESCE(df.feature_id, 0) as feature_id
    FROM daily_llm_calls dlc
    LEFT JOIN {{ ref('dim_llm_models') }} dm 
        ON dlc.provider = dm.provider 
        AND dlc.model = dm.model_name
    LEFT JOIN {{ ref('dim_features') }} df 
        ON LOWER(dlc.feature_name) = LOWER(df.feature_name)
)

SELECT
    call_date as date,
    provider,
    model_id,
    feature_id,
    total_tokens,
    total_prompt_tokens,
    total_completion_tokens,
    total_cost_usd,
    avg_cost_per_call,
    call_count,
    error_count,


### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços para V10

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

### CONTEXTO:
A V9 do DIYAPP atingiu limites de escalabilidade com arquitetura monolítica. O sistema precisa:
1. Suportar 10x mais usuários simultâneos
2. Permitir deploy independente de funcionalidades
3. Facilitar experimentação com diferentes modelos de IA
4. Manter estabilidade 100% autônoma

### DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços baseada em containers com os seguintes princípios:
- Cada serviço é independente e responsável por um domínio específico
- Comunicação via API REST para síncrono e mensageria para assíncrono
- Cada serviço tem seu próprio banco de dados
- API Gateway como ponto único de entrada
- Service Mesh para observabilidade e resiliência

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A**: Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simples deploy, debugging fácil. Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, acoplamento alto.
- **Opção B**: Microsserviços completos - Prós: Escalabilidade independente, resiliência. Contras: Complexidade operacional, latência de rede.
- **Opção C**: Arquitetura híbrida (microsserviços + módulos) - Prós: Balanceamento. Contras: Inconsistência arquitetural.

**Opção escolhida: B** - Justificativa: Necessidade de escalabilidade extrema e deploy independente justifica a complexidade adicional.

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Escalabilidade horizontal independente
- Deploy contínuo sem downtime
- Tecnologias heterogêneas por serviço
- Resiliência através de circuit breakers

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade de debugging distribuído
- Overhead de comunicação entre serviços
- Gerenciamento de transações distribuídas
- Custos operacionais mais altos

**Riscos:**
1. Latência acumulada - Mitigação: Cache distribuído e design assíncrono
2. Consistência eventual - Mitigação: Padrões SAGA e compensação
3. Observabilidade - Mitigação: Service Mesh com tracing completo

### REVISÃO: 2024-04-15

---

## 2. Engineering Standards - V10

```markdown
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V10

## 1. Estrutura de Repositório

diyapp-v10/

## 2. Padrões de Código

### 2.1 Linguagens Principais
- **Backend Services**: Node.js 20+ com TypeScript
- **API Gateway**: Go 1.21+ (performance crítica)
- **Scripts utilitários**: Python 3.11+

### 2.2 Convenções TypeScript
```typescript
// Nomenclatura
interface IUserService {}          // Interface prefixada com I
class UserRepository {}           // Classes em PascalCase
const MAX_RETRIES = 3;           // Constantes em UPPER_SNAKE_CASE
let userCount: number;           // Variáveis em camelCase

// Estrutura de arquivo
// 1. Imports (externos → internos)
// 2. Interfaces/Types
// 3. Constantes
// 4. Classes/Funções
// 5. Export

// Exemplo completo:
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { IUser, UserRole } from '@diyapp/shared-types';

const DEFAULT_PAGE_SIZE = 20;

export interface ICreateUserDto {
  email: string;
  password: string;
  role?: UserRole;
}

@Injectable()
export class UserService {
  constructor(private readonly userRepository: UserRepository) {}

  async createUser(dto: ICreateUserDto): Promise<IUser> {
    // Implementação
  }
}
```

### 2.3 Padrões de API REST
```
GET    /resources          - Listar com paginação
GET    /resources/{id}     - Obter por ID
POST   /resources          - Criar novo
PUT    /resources/{id}     - Substituir completo
PATCH  /resources/{id}     - Atualizar parcial
DELETE /resources/{id}     - Remover

// Headers obrigatórios:
X-Request-ID: uuid-v4      // Para tracing
X-User-ID: uuid-v4         // ID do usuário autenticado
X-API-Version: 1.0         // Versionamento
```

### 2.4 Versionamento Semântico
```
MAJOR.MINOR.PATCH
- MAJOR: Breaking changes na API
- MINOR: Novas funcionalidades compatíveis
- PATCH: Correções de bugs

// Exemplo no package.json:
{
  "name": "@diyapp/auth-service",
  "version": "1.2.3",
  "dependencies": {
    "@diyapp/shared-types": "^2.0.0",  // Compatível com 2.x.x
    "express": "~4.18.2"               // Compatível com 4.18.x
  }
}
```

### 2.5 Conventional Commits
```
<type>(<scope>): <description>

Types:
feat:     Nova funcionalidade
fix:      Correção de bug
docs:     Documentação
style:    Formatação (semântica)
refactor: Refatoração
test:     Testes
chore:    Tarefas de build/CI

Exemplos:
feat(auth): implementar login com OAuth2
fix(api): corrigir SQL injection na query de usuários
docs(readme): adicionar instruções de deploy
```

## 3. Estrutura de Serviço

Cada serviço segue:
```
service-name/
├── src/
│   ├── controllers/      # Handlers HTTP
│   ├── services/         # Lógica de negócio
│   ├── repositories/     # Acesso a dados
│   ├── models/          # Entidades/DTOs
│   ├── middleware/      # Middlewares específicos
│   ├── utils/           # Utilitários
│   └── index.ts         # Ponto de entrada
├── tests/
│   ├── unit/
│   ├── integration/
│   └── e2e/
├── Dockerfile
├── docker-compose.yml   # Para desenvolvimento
├── package.json
├── tsconfig.json
├── .env.example
└── README.md
```

## 4. Testes
- Cobertura mínima: 80%
- Testes unitários: Jest
- Testes de integração: Supertest + Docker
- E2E: Cypress para frontend, Newman para APIs

## 5. Segurança
- Scan de dependências: Snyk/Dependabot
- Secrets em HashiCorp Vault
- Rate limiting por serviço
- Input validation com Zod
- SQL parameterized queries apenas
```

---

```markdown
## Descrição
<!-- Descreva o que este PR faz -->

- [ ] Bug fix
- [ ] Nova funcionalidade
- [ ] Breaking change
- [ ] Refatoração
- [ ] Documentação

## Checklist
- [ ] Meu código segue os padrões do projeto
- [ ] Eu fiz review do meu próprio código
- [ ] Eu comentei meu código, especialmente em partes complexas
- [ ] Eu adicionei testes que provam que minha correção/funcionalidade funciona
- [ ] Testes novos e existentes passam localmente
- [ ] Qualquer mudança dependente foi mergeada e publicada

## Testes
<!-- Descreva os testes que você executou -->

## Screenshots (se aplicável)

## Contexto Adicional
<!-- Links para issues, ADRs relevantes, etc -->
```

### 3.2 .github/workflows/ci.yml
```yaml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  lint-and-test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, auth-service, llm-orchestrator, task-executor]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: '20'
        cache: 'npm'
        cache-dependency-path: services/${{ matrix.service }}/package-lock.json
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: npm ci
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Lint
      run: npm run lint
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Type check
      run: npm run type-check
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Run tests
      run: npm test -- --coverage
      working-directory: services/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Upload coverage
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: services/${{ matrix.service }}/coverage/lcov.info
        flags: ${{ matrix.service }}

  security-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint-and-test
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Run Snyk to check for vulnerabilities
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --severity-threshold=high
    
    - name: Run Trivy vulnerability scanner
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        scan-type: 'fs'
        scan-ref: '.'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
    
    - name: Upload Trivy scan results to GitHub Security tab
      uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
      with:
        sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'
```

### 3.3 .github/workflows/cd.yml
```yaml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  build-and-push:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, auth-service, llm-orchestrator, task-executor]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Set up Docker Buildx
      uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
    
    - name: Log in to Docker Hub
      uses: docker/login-action@v2
      with:
        username: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}
        password: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_PASSWORD }}
    
    - name: Extract metadata
      id: meta
      uses: docker/metadata-action@v4
      with:
        images: diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}
        tags: |
          type=ref,event=branch
          type=sha,prefix={{branch}}-
          type=semver,pattern={{version}}
    
    - name: Build and push
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
      with:
        context: services/${{ matrix.service }}
        push: true
        tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
        labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}
        cache-from: type=gha
        cache-to: type=gha,mode=max

  deploy-staging:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: build-and-push
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Configure Kubernetes
      run: |
        mkdir -p $HOME/.kube
        echo "${{ secrets.KUBE_CONFIG }}" > $HOME/.kube/config
    
    - name: Deploy to staging
      run: |
        kubectl config use-context staging
        kubectl apply -f infrastructure/k8s/staging/
        kubectl rollout status deployment/diyapp-api-gateway -n diyapp-staging
```

## 4. Docker Configuration

### 4.1 services/api-gateway/Dockerfile
```dockerfile
# Build stage
FROM golang:1.21-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

COPY go.mod go.sum ./
RUN go mod download

COPY . .
RUN CGO_ENABLED=0 GOOS=linux go build -a -installsuffix cgo -o main ./cmd/api-gateway

# Runtime stage
FROM alpine:latest

RUN apk --no-cache add ca-certificates tzdata
WORKDIR /root/

COPY --from=builder /app/main .
COPY --from=builder /app/.env.production .env

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD wget --no-verbose --tries=1 --spider http://localhost:8080/health || exit 1

EXPOSE 8080

CMD ["./main"]
```

### 4.2 services/auth-service/Dockerfile
```dockerfile
# Build stage
FROM node:20-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

COPY . .
RUN npm run build

# Runtime stage
FROM node:20-alpine

WORKDIR /app

RUN apk add --no-cache tzdata

COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder /app/package.json ./

USER node

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=10s --retries=3 \
  CMD node -e "require('http').get('http://localhost:3000/health', (r) => {process.exit(r.statusCode === 200 ? 0 : 1)})"

EXPOSE 3000

CMD ["node", "dist/index.js"]
```

### 4.3 infrastructure/docker-compose.yml
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # API Gateway
  api-gateway:
    build: ../services/api-gateway
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - AUTH_SERVICE_URL=http://auth-service:3000
      - LLM_SERVICE_URL=http://llm-orchestrator:3001
    depends_on:
      - auth-service
      - llm-orchestrator
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Auth Service
  auth-service:
    build: ../services/auth-service
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - DB_HOST=postgres-auth
      - DB_PORT=5432
      - DB_NAME=auth_db
      - DB_USER=auth_user
      - DB_PASSWORD=auth_password
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis-auth:6379
    depends_on:
      - postgres-auth
      - redis-auth
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # LLM Orchestrator
  llm-orchestrator:
    build: ../services/llm-orchestrator
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY}
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis-llm:6379
      - RABBITMQ_URL=amqp://rabbitmq:5672
    depends_on:
      - redis-llm
      - rabbitmq
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Databases
  postgres-auth:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=auth_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=auth_user
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=auth_password
    volumes:
      - postgres-auth-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Redis instances
  redis-auth:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-server --requirepass redis_password
    volumes:
      - redis-auth-data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  redis-llm:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-server --requirepass redis_password
    volumes:
      - redis-llm-data:/data
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # Message Queue


### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Design e UI

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes premium e wireframes de alta fidelidade para o dashboard principal e fluxos de automação.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-design-system/
├── index.html              # Dashboard principal
├── design-tokens.js        # Sistema de tokens de design
├── style.css              # Estilos globais e utilitários
├── components/            # Componentes UI reutilizáveis
│   ├── button.js
│   ├── card.js
│   ├── modal.js
│   ├── navigation.js
│   └── form-elements.js
├── pages/                 # Wireframes de alta fidelidade
│   ├── dashboard.html
│   ├── automation.html
│   └── settings.html
└── assets/
    ├── icons/
    └── fonts/
```

## 1. Sistema de Tokens de Design (design-tokens.js)

```javascript
// design-tokens.js
class DesignTokens {
  constructor() {
    this.tokens = {
      version: 'v1.0.0',
      lastUpdated: new Date().toISOString(),
      
      // Cores - Sistema de cores com tokens semânticos
      colors: {
        // Primárias
        primary: {
          50: '#e6f7ff',
          100: '#bae7ff',
          200: '#91d5ff',
          300: '#69c0ff',
          400: '#40a9ff',
          500: '#1890ff', // Primary Main
          600: '#096dd9',
          700: '#0050b3',
          800: '#003a8c',
          900: '#002766'
        },
        
        // Neutros para light/dark mode
        neutral: {
          50: '#fafafa',
          100: '#f5f5f5',
          200: '#e8e8e8',
          300: '#d9d9d9',
          400: '#bfbfbf',
          500: '#8c8c8c',
          600: '#595959',
          700: '#434343',
          800: '#262626',
          900: '#1f1f1f'
        },
        
        // Estados
        success: {
          light: '#f6ffed',
          main: '#52c41a',
          dark: '#237804',
          contrast: '#ffffff'
        },
        warning: {
          light: '#fffbe6',
          main: '#faad14',
          dark: '#ad6800',
          contrast: '#ffffff'
        },
        error: {
          light: '#fff2f0',
          main: '#ff4d4f',
          dark: '#a8071a',
          contrast: '#ffffff'
        },
        info: {
          light: '#e6f7ff',
          main: '#1890ff',
          dark: '#0050b3',
          contrast: '#ffffff'
        },
        
        // Backgrounds
        background: {
          light: {
            default: '#ffffff',
            paper: '#fafafa',
            elevated: '#ffffff',
            subtle: '#f5f5f5'
          },
          dark: {
            default: '#1a1a1a',
            paper: '#262626',
            elevated: '#2a2a2a',
            subtle: '#1f1f1f'
          }
        },
        
        // Texto
        text: {
          light: {
            primary: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.87)',
            secondary: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6)',
            disabled: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.38)',
            hint: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.38)'
          },
          dark: {
            primary: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.95)',
            secondary: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.7)',
            disabled: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)',
            hint: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.5)'
          }
        }
      },
      
      // Tipografia - Escala modular
      typography: {
        fontFamily: {
          primary: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
          mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'Courier New', monospace"
        },
        fontSize: {
          xs: '0.75rem',    // 12px
          sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
          base: '1rem',     // 16px
          lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px
          xl: '1.25rem',    // 20px
          '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
          '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
          '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
          '5xl': '3rem'      // 48px
        },
        fontWeight: {
          light: 300,
          normal: 400,
          medium: 500,
          semibold: 600,
          bold: 700
        },
        lineHeight: {
          tight: 1.25,
          normal: 1.5,
          relaxed: 1.75
        }
      },
      
      // Espaçamento - Escala 8px
      spacing: {
        0: '0',
        1: '0.25rem',   // 4px
        2: '0.5rem',    // 8px
        3: '0.75rem',   // 12px
        4: '1rem',      // 16px
        5: '1.25rem',   // 20px
        6: '1.5rem',    // 24px
        8: '2rem',      // 32px
        10: '2.5rem',   // 40px
        12: '3rem',     // 48px
        16: '4rem',     // 64px
        20: '5rem',     // 80px
        24: '6rem'      // 96px
      },
      
      // Border Radius
      borderRadius: {
        none: '0',
        sm: '0.125rem',   // 2px
        base: '0.25rem',  // 4px
        md: '0.375rem',   // 6px
        lg: '0.5rem',     // 8px
        xl: '0.75rem',    // 12px
        '2xl': '1rem',    // 16px
        '3xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
        full: '9999px'
      },
      
      // Elevação (Box Shadows)
      elevation: {
        0: 'none',
        1: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
        2: '0 1px 3px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
        3: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
        4: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
        5: '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04)',
        inner: 'inset 0 2px 4px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)'
      },
      
      // Transições
      transition: {
        duration: {
          fast: '150ms',
          normal: '250ms',
          slow: '350ms'
        },
        timing: {
          ease: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
          easeIn: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)',
          easeOut: 'cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)',
          easeInOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)'
        }
      },
      
      // Breakpoints responsivos
      breakpoints: {
        xs: '320px',
        sm: '640px',
        md: '768px',
        lg: '1024px',
        xl: '1280px',
        '2xl': '1536px'
      }
    };
    
    this.currentTheme = 'light';
    this.init();
  }
  
  init() {
    this.applyTheme();
    this.generateCSSVariables();
  }
  
  toggleTheme() {
    this.currentTheme = this.currentTheme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light';
    this.applyTheme();
    return this.currentTheme;
  }
  
  applyTheme() {
    const root = document.documentElement;
    const theme = this.currentTheme;
    
    // Aplicar cores do tema
    Object.entries(this.tokens.colors.background[theme]).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--color-background-${key}`, value);
    });
    
    Object.entries(this.tokens.colors.text[theme]).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--color-text-${key}`, value);
    });
    
    // Aplicar cores comuns
    Object.entries(this.tokens.colors.primary).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--color-primary-${key}`, value);
    });
    
    // Definir tema atual
    root.setAttribute('data-theme', theme);
  }
  
  generateCSSVariables() {
    const root = document.documentElement;
    
    // Gerar todas as variáveis CSS
    Object.entries(this.tokens).forEach(([category, values]) => {
      if (category === 'colors') return; // Já aplicado no applyTheme
      
      this.flattenObject(values, `--${category}`).forEach(([key, value]) => {
        root.style.setProperty(key, value);
      });
    });
  }
  
  flattenObject(obj, prefix = '') {
    return Object.entries(obj).reduce((acc, [key, value]) => {
      const newKey = prefix ? `${prefix}-${key}` : `--${key}`;
      
      if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
        acc.push(...this.flattenObject(value, newKey));
      } else {
        acc.push([newKey, value]);
      }
      
      return acc;
    }, []);
  }
  
  getToken(path) {
    return path.split('.').reduce((obj, key) => obj?.[key], this.tokens);
  }
  
  exportTokens() {
    return JSON.stringify(this.tokens, null, 2);
  }
}

// Instância global
window.DesignTokens = new DesignTokens();
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Microsserviço Core e Automação

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-core/
├── packages/
│   ├── core-service/          # Microsserviço Core (API Gateway + Auth + Logs)
│   └── automation-service/    # Microsserviço de Automação (Orquestrador de Tarefas)
├── docker-compose.yml
├── .env.example
└── README.md
```

## 1. Configuração do Ambiente (docker-compose.yml)

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Redis para filas e cache
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3

  # PostgreSQL para dados persistentes
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-diyapp123}
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_core
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init-db.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3

  # Core Service
  core-service:
    build: ./packages/core-service
    container_name: diyapp-core
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      PORT: 3000
      JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET:-your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production}
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:${DB_PASSWORD:-diyapp123}@postgres:5432/diyapp_core
      LOG_LEVEL: info
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "node", "healthcheck.js"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # Automation Service
  automation-service:
    build: ./packages/automation-service
    container_name: diyapp-automation
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:${DB_PASSWORD:-diyapp123}@postgres:5432/diyapp_core
      WORKER_CONCURRENCY: 5
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs

volumes:
  redis_data:
  postgres_data:
```

## 2. Script de Inicialização do Banco (init-db.sql)

```sql
-- Tabela de usuários
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    role VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'user',
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    last_login TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Tabela de refresh tokens
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS refresh_tokens (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    token VARCHAR(500) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    expires_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    revoked BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_refresh_tokens_token (token),
    INDEX idx_refresh_tokens_user_id (user_id)
);

-- Tabela de logs centralizados
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS system_logs (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    level VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    service VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    correlation_id VARCHAR(100),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    endpoint VARCHAR(500),
    method VARCHAR(10),
    status_code INTEGER,
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    message TEXT NOT NULL,
    metadata JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Tabela de tarefas de automação
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS automation_tasks (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    job_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'pending',
    payload JSONB NOT NULL,
    result JSONB,
    error TEXT,
    attempts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    max_attempts INTEGER DEFAULT 3,
    scheduled_for TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    started_at TIMESTAMP,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    INDEX idx_automation_tasks_status (status),
    INDEX idx_automation_tasks_scheduled_for (scheduled_for),
    INDEX idx_automation_tasks_job_id (job_id)
);

-- Tabela de workflows
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS automation_workflows (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    trigger_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    trigger_config JSONB NOT NULL,
    steps JSONB NOT NULL,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    last_executed TIMESTAMP,
    execution_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    success_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    failure_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Criar usuário admin padrão (senha: admin123)
INSERT INTO users (id, email, password_hash, name, role) 
VALUES (
    'a0eebc99-9c0b-4ef8-bb6d-6bb9bd380a11',
    'admin@diyapp.com',
    '$2b$10$92IXUNpkjO0rOQ5byMi.Ye4oKoEa3Ro9llC/.og/at2.uheWG/igi', -- bcrypt hash de "admin123"
    'Administrator',
    'admin'
) ON CONFLICT (email) DO NOTHING;

-- Criar índices para performance
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_system_logs_correlation_id ON system_logs(correlation_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_system_logs_created_at ON system_logs(created_at);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_system_logs_service_level ON system_logs(service, level);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_automation_tasks_created_at ON automation_tasks(created_at);
```

## 3. Pacote Core Service

  "scripts": {
    "start": "node src/index.js",
    "dev": "nodemon src/index.js",
    "test": "jest",
